 On Tuesday, Chief Justice Deepak Mishra administered the oath of office to Justice Indira Banerjee, Justice Vineet Saran and Justice KM Joseph in a traditional ceremony
 inamen se justise ke em joseph kii niyukti ko lekar vivaad tha ki isamen varishthata kaa dhyaan nahin rakhaa gaya or unhen is suchi main tisare sthaan par rakhaa gaya he, jabaki essi collegium main unhen top par rakhaa tha
 Let us know how seniority is decided in the Supreme Court and what was the controversy
 
 
 kya tha vivadasbase pehle yah bataate hai ki is bare main vivaad kya he? asal main collegium ne uttarakhand hai court ke chif justise rahe justise joseph ko supreme court kaa jaj banane ke liye gat 10 janvari ko sifarish kii thi
 Apart from him, senior advocate Indu Malhotra was also named
 lekin sarkaar ne april main malhotra kii niyukti kaa warrant jari kar diya or justise joseph kaa naam waapas kar diya
 After this, on 16 July, the collegium again extended the name of Justice Joseph and named two other names along with him, Justice Indira Banerjee and Justice Vineet Saran
 sarkaar ne pichley hafte teenon jajon kii niyukti ke liye warrant to jari kar diya, lekin justise joseph ko kram main justise banerjee or justise saran ke baad sthaan diya gaya, jiskaa matlab yah he ki vah ukt donon jajon se junior ho gaye, jabaki unke liye sifarish donon jajon se pehle kii gai thi
 Many Supreme Court judges feel that the government has violated the established procedure for fixing seniority
 justise joseph ko chif justise ke liye mana tha sabase yogyaindian express akhbaar ke mutabik kalegium ne kaha tha, 'justise joseph sabhi lihaaj se supreme court kaa chif justise banane ke liye hoicourt ke sabhi jajon se varisht or yogya tathaa upyukt ummidavaar hai
 'how seniority is decided in the Supreme Court? The seniority of the judges is decided on the basis of the date and oath taken in the Supreme Court
 yani jis jaj ne pehle shapath liya vah baaki baad main shapath lene vaale jajon se senior hua
 Actually, there is no set rule in this regard
 yah bhi saaf nahin he ki agar kai jaj ek hi tithi main shapath lete hai to unki varishthata kaa nirnay kaise ho
 The government issues warrants for it in an order, then according to the order in which the warrant is issued before it is sworn in
 udhaaharan ke liye maujuuda chif justise deepak mishra or ritred justise je chelmeshwar kii niyukti kaa aadesh ek hi tithi kaa tha, lekin mishra kaa warrant kram main chelmeshwar se pehle tha, isliye unhone pehle shapath liya or unhen chelmeshchar se senior mana gaya
 On this basis, he also became Chief Justice
 jajon kii niyukti ke liye warrant collegium kii sifarish ke aadhaar par jari hota he, jisamen supreme court ke paanch varisht jaj hote hai
 But the final decision is issued by the government

 Former Union Finance Minister Yashwant Sinha, who questioned economic policy, has been hit by Finance Minister Arun Jaitley
 jetali ne sinha ko 80 saal kii umr main naukari chaahane vaala qaraar dete hue kaha ki vah vitt mantri ke rup main apane record ko bhul gaye hai
 In this case, Sinha's son and Union Minister of State for Civil Aviation Jayant Sinha also jumped in and vigorously defended the government's economic policies
 ek pustak vimochan kaarykram main jetali ne kaha ki sinha nitiyon kii bajaay vyaktiyon par tippanee kar rahe hai
 He alleged that Yashwant Sinha was following senior Congress leader and former Finance Minister p Chidambaram
 vah bhul chuke hai ki kaise kabhi donon ek-duusare ke khilaaf kadave bol kaa istemaal karte the
 However, Jaitley did not directly name Sinha, but said that he did not have the privilege of being the former finance minister, nor did he have the privilege of being a former finance minister who has become a columnist today, in this Jaitley's first Mention was for Sinha and another for Chidambaram
 unhone kaha ki purv vitt mantri hone par main aasaani se upie do main nitigat shithilataa ko bhul jaataa
 i would have easily forgotten the 1998 to 2002 npas
 us samay sinha vitt mantri the
 i would have easily forgotten the four billion dollar foreign exchange reserves left in 1991
 main paala badalakar isaki vyakhya badal detaa
 Jaitley lashed out at Sinha and said that he was looking for a job through such comments
 sirf peeche-peeche chalane se tathy nahin badal jaaenge

 Dr
 Ram Manohar Lohia was one of the few politicians in the country whose intellectualism and impudence and simplistic life had deeply influenced the public
 gandhi, nehru, ambedkar, jepi kii tarah lohia kaa bhi janamanas par gadha asar tha
 He fought more in independent India than he fought in the national movement and was also jailed many times
 nehru ke ve sabase bade aalochak the or samaaj kii sabhi samasyaon par krantikari dhang se vichaar kiya tha
 No one has as much dialogue as he had with Hindi writers
 unhone ucch koti ke niabandh bhi likhe or yaadgaar tathaa prabhaavshaalee bhaashan bhi die
 The late Mastram Kapoor edited his Rachnavali a few years ago and did a good job for the readers of Hindi, but there was no such book for the general readers, which could read all the major ideas of Lohia at one place
 prasiddh patrkaar ke
 Vikram Rao and young scholar Pradeep Kumar Singh have done the work for the general readers and Lohia lovers by removing Lohia accumulation
 573 pannon kii is kitaab main gaagar main sagar bharne kaa kaam kiya gaya he
 This is more beneficial for the younger generation as this single book will show them all aspects of Lohia's ideological personality
 aath adhyyon vaali is kitaab main marxvad, gandhivaad, samaajwaad, dharm, darshan, bhashaa, jati or stri ke prashn se lekar videsh niti, kashmir kaa sawaal or sansadeey raajnneeti, paryaavaran or shiksha sabhi vishyon par lohia ke lekh shaamil kiye gaye hai
 Apart from his famous essays like Ram, Krishna, Shiva, Draupadi and Savitri, his articles, letters, book reviews and speeches on English Hatao and Ramayana Mela are also included
 unki charchit pustak bharat vibhaajan ke apradhi ke ek ansh ko bhi shaamil kiya gaya he, jo unhone moulana aaazaad kii pustak india vins freedom kii samiksha karte hue likhi thi
 Lohia also debated "nehru ji is the world's most expensive Prime Minister" in Parliament
 use bhi shaamil kiya gaya he
 The book thus gives a complete picture of Lohia and a glimpse of his talent
